Result: 原初黑洞的无量纲自旋可达χ∼0.1-1，远超过潮汐扭矩理论预测，当小尺度功率谱增强时可产生可探测丰度

Conclusion: 建立了暴胀、原初扰动和黑洞自旋分布之间的可测试联系，为引力波观测提供了新的理论框架

Abstract: The origin of cosmic angular momentum is a fundamental question in structure formation. We propose a novel mechanism that generates spatial angular momentum directly from quantum fluctuations during inflation. A spectator complex scalar field with global U(1) symmetry stores internal angular momentum via field-space rotation. Inflationary perturbations create spatial gradients that, upon horizon re-entry, couple to the background charge density and source a bulk momentum flow. During nonspherical gravitational collapse, this flow converts into net angular momentum. For primordial black holes forming from such collapse, the dimensionless spin can reach \(χ\sim 0.1-1\) when the small-scale power spectrum is enhanced to produce detectable abundances-far exceeding tidal torque theory predictions. This establishes a testable link between inflation, primordial perturbations, and black hole spin distributions accessible to gravitational-wave observations.

</details>


### [382] [Spectral Bifurcations in Quasinormal Modes of Regular BTZ Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.14872)
*Kartheek Hegde,Tajron Jurić,A. Naveena Kumara*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究正则化BTZ黑洞中无质量标量场的准正规模谱，发现正则化保持线性稳定性但导致谱分支和模式重排


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索正则化BTZ黑洞的准正规模谱特性，了解几何正则化如何影响黑洞的动力学响应和稳定性

Method: 使用Leaver连分式方法和Horowitz-Hubeny幂级数方法计算标量准正规模，两种方法在参数空间内高度一致

Result: 正则化保持线性稳定性（ω_I < 0），但随着正则化尺度ℓ增加，BTZ类复分支与虚轴碰撞并分叉为多个纯虚分支，导致模式切换和泛音重排

Conclusion: 正则化BTZ黑洞展现出分叉准正规模谱，为研究谱分支和晚期衰落的几何机制提供了受控的(2+1)维平台

Abstract: We study the quasinormal spectrum of massless scalar fields propagating on a family of regular BTZ black holes arising from an infinite tower of dimensionally regularized Lovelock corrections. These geometries are asymptotically AdS, reduce to the standard BTZ solution in the limit $\ell \to 0$, and resolve the central singularity by introducing a smooth core controlled by the new length scale $\ell$. The scalar quasinormal modes are computed using both Leaver's continued-fraction method and the Horowitz-Hubeny power-series method; the two approaches agree to high accuracy across the parameter space. We find that the regularization preserves linear stability ($ω_I < 0$) while qualitatively reshaping the spectrum: as $\ell$ increases, BTZ-like complex branches collide with the imaginary axis and undergo a hierarchy of bifurcations into multiple purely imaginary branches, leading to mode switching and a nontrivial reordering of overtones as functions of $\ell$ and the harmonic index $m$. Our results place regular BTZ black holes within the emerging family of bifurcating quasinormal spectra known from nearly extremal and asymptotically AdS black holes, and highlight these $(2+1)$-dimensional geometries as a controlled arena for exploring geometric mechanisms behind spectral branching and late-time ringdown in regular black hole spacetimes.

</details>


### [383] [Parametrizing superfluid dark matter with rational approximations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15053)
*Francesco Lottatori*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究空间调制的实标量背景场如何影响超流体暗物质中的声子传播，发现正耦合会抑制声速平方，可能导致暗物质核心结构变化和形成不均匀区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超流体暗物质模型中，空间调制的标量背景场对声子传播的影响，理解这种调制如何改变暗物质介质的声速和刚性，从而影响暗物质核心的结构形成。

Method: 使用具有四次凝聚和耦合项-gφ²|Ψ|²的简单玩具模型，推导局部状态方程和有效声速c_s(x)。通过Padé径向剖面实现背景标量场的空间调制，分析不同耦合常数g下声速平方c_s²(r)的变化。

Result: 对于g>0，调制会增加凝聚的有效质量，使介质刚性降低，抑制声速平方c_s²∝m_{Ψ,eff}^{-4}，直至接近"尘埃状"状态(c_s²→0)。通过Padé剖面展示了c_s²(r)随径向距离的变化。

Conclusion: 空间调制的标量背景场能显著改变超流体暗物质中的声子传播特性，正耦合会抑制声速，这可能影响暗物质核心的结构，并可能导致暗物质不均匀区域的形成。

Abstract: We investigate how a spatially modulated real scalar background $φ(\vec{x})$ can modify phonon propagation in the context of Superfluid dark matter (SFDM). Using a simple toy model with quartic condensate and coupling $-gφ^2|Ψ|^2$, we derive the local equation of state and the effective sound velocity $c_s(\vec{x})$. For $g>0$, modulation tends to increase the effective mass of the condensate and make the medium less rigid, suppressing $c_s^2\propto m_{Ψ,\mathrm{eff}}^{-4}$ up to a ``dust-like'' regime, $c_s^2\to 0$. We implement this modulation for the background scalar field by imposing rational profiles, through Padé radial profiles, and show the corresponding variation of $c_s^2(r)$ for different $g$, discussing implications for the structure of SFDM cores and the possible formation of inhomogeneous regions of dark matter.

</details>


### [384] [The peculiar case of the Viaggiu holographic dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15067)
*Somnath Saha,Subhajit Saha,Nilanjana Mahata*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 研究基于Viaggiu熵的holographic dark energy模型，使用Hubble视界和未来事件视界作为特征尺度，发现可能存在的宇宙末日场景，结果与其他HDE模型形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Viaggiu熵（Bekenstein-Hawking熵的推广，包含膨胀宇宙中动态视界的额外项）在holographic dark energy模型中的适用性，研究这种新HDE模型在宇宙演化中的表现。

Method: 在平坦FLRW宇宙中，考虑暗物质（尘埃形式）和由Viaggiu熵产生的全息暗能量两种宇宙流体，分别以Hubble视界和未来事件视界作为特征长度尺度，研究宇宙演化。

Result: 分析揭示了有趣发现：包括未来可能存在的宇宙末日场景，某些观测结果与文献中其他HDE模型形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 基于Viaggiu熵的HDE模型显示出独特的宇宙演化特征，特别是预测了可能的宇宙末日，这与其他HDE模型不同，为暗能量研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the plausibility of a holographic dark energy (HDE) model using the form of horizon entropy proposed by Viaggiu in 2014. This form of entropy is a generalization of the usual Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, having an extra term arising due to the dynamical nature of horizons in an expanding universe. We examine this new HDE model in the context of a flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker universe filled with two cosmic fluids -- dark matter in the form of dust and holographic dark energy generated by Viaggiu entropy. We consider the Hubble horizon and the future event horizon as characteristic length scales and study the evolution of the Universe within these frameworks. Our analysis reveals some intriguing findings that include a possible cosmic doomsday scenario in the future, and certain observations are in striking contrast to other HDE models studied in the literature.

### [385] [Viaggiu holographic dark energy in light of DESI DR2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15178)
*Amlan K. Halder,Andronikos Paliathanasis,Stefano Viaggiu,Abdulla Al Mamon,Subhajit Saha*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Viaggiu全息暗能量模型(VHDE)通过晚期宇宙观测数据检验，结果显示其拟合效果与ΛCDM相当或更好，参数约束合理，但贝叶斯证据显示数据对ΛCDM有轻微偏好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试Viaggiu全息暗能量(VHDE)模型的宇宙学可行性，评估其作为ΛCDM替代模型描述晚期宇宙加速膨胀的能力。

Method: 使用多种晚期宇宙观测数据集：PantheonPlus、Union3.0、DES-Dovekie超新星数据，宇宙计时器，以及DESI DR2的重子声学振荡数据。通过参数约束分析，并采用Akaike信息准则(AIC)和贝叶斯证据进行模型比较。

Result: VHDE模型在所有数据集组合下拟合效果与ΛCDM相当或更好；H₀值与ΛCDM相似；当前物质密度参数Ωₘ₀≈0.24，小于ΛCDM结果；VHDE参数π/3δ²≈0.27-0.33；AIC显示两模型统计上不可区分，但贝叶斯证据显示数据对ΛCDM有轻微偏好。

Conclusion: VHDE模型与当前晚期宇宙观测数据一致，为描述晚期加速膨胀提供了可行机制，但与ΛCDM相比没有明显统计优势。

Abstract: We test the cosmological viability of the Viaggiu holographic dark energy (VHDE) model by using late-time observational data. In particular, we place constraints on the free parameters of the model using Type Ia supernovae from the PantheonPlus, Union3.0, and DES-Dovekie catalogues, the Cosmic Chronometers, and the Baryon Acoustic Oscillations from the DESI DR2. Our analysis suggests that the VHDE model fits the observational data better or similar to the $Λ$CDM for all dataset combinations considered. The value obtained for $H_0$ is similar to the $Λ$CDM, while the current matter density parameter is constrained around $Ω_{m0}\simeq 0.24$, smaller to that obtained by the $Λ$CDM. Moreover, the parameter introduced by the VHDE is found to have a mean value within the range $\fracπ{3} δ^2 \sim 0.27-0.33$. Finally, we used Akaike's Information Criterion (AIC) and Bayesian evidence to test the VHDE model against the $Λ$CDM scenario. The AIC demonstrates that the two models are statistically indistinguishable, while Bayesian evidence reveals that the data have a mild preference for the $Λ$CDM model for most of the dataset combinations considered. Nevertheless, the VHDE model remains consistent with current late-time cosmological observations and offers a feasible mechanism for describing the late-time accelerating scenario.

</details>
